Interpretation: for T(2,q) torus knots, the pq+1 hypothesis is tested
only when the relaxed candidate starts near |Q_H|=2q+1 and HOLDS
that charge. A seed close to some other integer sector is not a pq+1
test. Twist/non-torus knots are explicitly out of scope for pq+1.
For the energy-minimal-sector claim, relax several framings and compare
E only among runs that remain in their starting topological sector.
